RUS_CMA = {
	RUS_SALVATION_COMMITTEE = {
		icon = RUS_salvation_committee

		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 50
		days_remove = 15

		available = {
			original_tag = RUS
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = kherson_control_tt
				OR = {
					controls_state = 264
					controls_state = 262
					controls_state = 240
					controls_state = 251
					controls_state = 253
					controls_state = 231
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			original_tag = RUS
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision RUS_SALVATION_COMMITTEE"
		    if = {
				limit = { RUS = { controls_state = 264 } }
				264 = { add_compliance = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { controls_state = 262 } }
				262 = { add_compliance = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { controls_state = 240 } }
				240 = { add_compliance = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { controls_state = 251 } }
				251 = { add_compliance = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { controls_state = 253 } }
				253 = {	add_compliance = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { controls_state = 231 } }
				231 = { add_compliance = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { controls_state = 269 } }
				269 = { add_compliance = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { controls_state = 276 } }
				276 = { add_compliance = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { controls_state = 291 } }
				291 = { add_compliance = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { controls_state = 289 } }
				289 = {	add_compliance = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { controls_state = 266 } }
				266 = { add_compliance = 5 }
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = CMA_COMMITTEE
			}
		}
	}

		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 40
		available = {
			tag = RUS
		}
		visible = {
			tag = RUS
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_military_personnel }
			has_completed_focus = RUS_loyal_military_journalists
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision RUS_military_personnel_bet"
		    custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_military_personnel_bet_cet
		    hidden_effect = {
			    if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = RUS_psychological_operation
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = RUS_monthly_increase_var_add value = -1.5 }
					UKR = {
						remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_propaganda_debuff }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = RUS_internal_support
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = RUS_monthly_increase_var_add value = 1.5 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = RUS_war_on_fakes
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = RUS_monthly_increase_var_add value = -2 }
				}
			    clr_country_flag = RUS_internal_support
				clr_country_flag = RUS_war_on_fakes
				clr_country_flag = RUS_psychological_operation
				set_country_flag = RUS_military_personnel
				clear_variable = RUS_inf_war_making_bet_political_power_factor
				clear_variable = RUS_inf_war_making_bet_political_power_cost
				clear_variable = RUS_inf_war_making_bet_stability_factor
				clear_variable = RUS_inf_war_making_bet_war_support_factor
				clear_variable = RUS_inf_war_making_bet_weekly_manpower
				clear_variable = RUS_inf_war_making_bet_training_time_army_factor
				clear_variable = RUS_inf_war_making_bet_command_power_gain_mult
				add_to_variable = { var = RUS_inf_war_making_bet_war_support_factor value = 0.075 }
				add_to_variable = { var = RUS_inf_war_making_bet_weekly_manpower value = 100 }
				add_to_variable = { var = RUS_inf_war_making_bet_command_power_gain_mult value = 0.05 }
			}
		}

		icon = GFX_SMO_Negotiations
		
		cost = 10
		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 2

		visible = {}

		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SMO_prisoners_of_war_exchange_started_RUS_trigger
				has_global_flag = SMO_prisoner_of_war_exchange_gf
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SMO_exchange_prisoners_of_war_25_RUS_trigger
				check_variable = { RUS.prisoners_of_war_captured_by_UKR > 24 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SMO_exchange_prisoners_of_war_25_UKR_trigger
				check_variable = { UKR.prisoners_of_war_captured_by_RUS > 24 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SMO_exchange_prisoners_soon_gf_trigger
				has_global_flag = {
					flag = SMO_exchange_prisoners_soon_gf
					days > 14
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision SMO_exchange_prisoners_of_war_25: complete_effect"
			clr_global_flag = SMO_exchange_prisoners_soon_gf
			set_global_flag = SMO_exchange_prisoners_soon_gf
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision SMO_exchange_prisoners_of_war_25: remove_effect"
			custom_effect_tooltip = SMO_exchange_prisoners_of_war_25_cet
			RUS = { add_stability = 0.012 }
			UKR = { add_stability = 0.012 }
			hidden_effect = {
				RUS = { 
					subtract_from_variable = { prisoners_of_war_captured_by_UKR = 25 }
					add_to_variable = { new_returned_prisoners_of_war_k = 0.025 }
				}
